posted:Posted March 25, 2022
msg:This stay was booked 3 days in advance. When booking, please note that you need a twin room with a river view on a high floor. Two days before check-in, the hotel staff called and told me that they had upgraded the room type, but they could only meet the requirements of double beds and high floors, which could not be satisfied by the river view. I said that there is no need to change to a double room, it does not matter if there is no river view. On the morning of the check-in day, I called the hotel again, and wanted to try to ask if I could meet all of my requirements, but this time the front desk said that I could apply for a room upgrade, so that the requirements of Jiangjing could also be met.

We checked in after 7 pm. On the way to the hotel, we passed the Cherry Blossom Avenue by the river. The scenery is very good, but unfortunately we didn't come to enjoy the beautiful scenery during the day. Because it was during the epidemic and because we arrived late, there were no other guests in the lobby when we checked in. Our check-in was handled by Ivy at the front desk. She told us that the room had been upgraded to the Supreme River View Twin Room on the 20th floor, which is 2 floors higher than the 18th floor mentioned on the phone before, and added WeChat to inform me about the hotel. He also said that if you have any questions, you can contact her directly on WeChat. Since we were staying at this hotel for the first time, Ivy personally took us to the elevator entrance and sent us into the elevator before leaving.

The room is large, with 50 square meters. There are two bottles of mineral water in the room, tea bags from TWG, and two packets of instant coffee. There are also two bottles of water in the small refrigerator, as well as cola, herbal tea, beer and coconut milk. I saw a lot of people in the comments saying that the small refrigerator is free, but I was not sure, so I asked Ivy on WeChat, and I got an immediate reply that it was free. In addition, before I checked in, I asked for two more bottles of water on the phone. The front desk replied that if I finished drinking, I would ask the hotel for it, but in fact, shortly after we checked in, the front desk sent someone to deliver two bottles of water, and the service attitude was still very good. OK. There is a long sofa by the window in the room, which can even sleep one person. The bathroom area is also large. The shower room and the toilet are separated from each other, and there is a distance from the sink. In addition, there is a bathtub by the window. There is a shelf above the bathtub, so you can put things in the bath. You can see the river view directly from the windows in the room and bathroom. Because the room is high floor and close to the river, you don't have to worry about being seen by outsiders when you take a bath. The TV in the room has a look back function, which is not available in many hotel TVs. However, we still encountered a little problem after our stay. When I took a shower, I found that the sewer in the shower room was blocked. After taking a shower, I opened the door of the shower room, and the water flowed outside. I called the front desk to report the situation, and the front desk immediately sent someone to repair the sewer, and asked the cleaner to clean up the accumulated water. The efficiency of solving the problem is very high. After the problem was solved, I took a bath in the bathtub, put my mobile phone on the shelf to watch a drama, and looked out the window from time to time to enjoy the river view. After soaking for more than an hour, it can be said to be very comfortable. Because the quilt and mattress are relatively thick, we turned on the air conditioner to 18 degrees when we went to bed, so that we didn't feel hot, and both of us slept very soundly all night.

After getting up the next day, we went to the restaurant on the first floor for breakfast. Looking at the reviews before, many people said that the restaurant on the 28th floor can also have breakfast, and the scenery is very good, but this time the front desk did not mention it, probably because the restaurant on the 28th floor was not open due to the epidemic. But that's okay, because it rained a lot the next morning and couldn't enjoy the view even from the 28th floor. The restaurant on the ground floor is very large and the food is plentiful, both of us were very full. After eating, we went back to the room to rest for a while, and then went downstairs to check out when the rain was a little lighter, ending our hotel tour.

Staying for one night this time, I have a very good impression of this hotel, whether it is the location, facilities or services, they are very good. Especially the front desk Ivy who is in charge of receiving us, the service attitude is very good, if you have any questions, you can reply immediately, here is a big like. If there is a chance in the future, I will visit again.
